   (function(userDB) {
        var initialized;
        var done = function() {
            if (!initialized) {
                initialized = true;
                timerId && clearTimeout(timerId);
                if (window.Connext && window.Connext.Run) {
                    window.Connext.Run();
                } else {
                    // wait for Connext to load
                    var timerIdPoll = setInterval(function() {
                        if (window.Connext && window.Connext.Run) {
                            clearInterval(timerIdPoll);
                            window.Connext.Run();
                        }
                    }, 500);
                }
            }
        };
        var timerId = setTimeout(function() {
            done();
        }, 3000);
        (window.top._matherq = window.top._matherq || []).push(['getTracker', function(tracker) {
            tracker.setPaywall('mg2');
            if (userDB) {
                tracker.getUserDBSegment({}, function(userDBData) {
                done();
                });
            } else {
                done();
            }
        }]);
    })(true);

  <script>
   $(function($) {
    var num_cols = 2,
    container = $('.dropdown .dropdown-menu .col-sm-2 .list-unstyled'),
    listItem = 'li',
    listClass = 'sub-list';
    container.each(function() {
        var items_per_col = new Array(),
        items = $(this).find(listItem),
        min_items_per_col = Math.floor(items.length / num_cols),
        difference = items.length - (min_items_per_col * num_cols);
        for (var i = 0; i < num_cols; i++) {
            if (i < difference) {
                items_per_col[i] = min_items_per_col + 1;
            } else {
                items_per_col[i] = min_items_per_col;
            }
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < num_cols; i++) {
            $(this).append($('<ul ></ul>').addClass(listClass));
            for (var j = 0; j < items_per_col[i]; j++) {
                var pointer = 0;
                for (var k = 0; k < i; k++) {
                    pointer += items_per_col[k];
                }
                $(this).find('.' + listClass).last().append(items[j + pointer]);
            }
        }
    });
});
  </script>

        function delete_cookie(name) {
            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";
            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;domain="+location.host+";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";

            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;domain=."+rootdomain+";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";

            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;domain="+location.host+";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";

            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;domain="+rootdomain+";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";
            document.cookie = name + "=;path=/;domain=."+rootdomain+";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";

          <script>
           var gazetteNotificationsBell    = $('#gazette-bell-container');
    var gazetteNotificationsDrawer  = $('#notificationsDrawer');

    function toggleDrawer() {
        if (gazetteNotificationsDrawer.hasClass('showDrawer')) {
            gazetteNotificationsDrawer.hide('slide', {
                'direction':    'right'
            }, 500).addClass('hideDrawer').removeClass('showDrawer');
        } else {
            gazetteNotificationsDrawer.show('slide', {
                'direction':    'right'
            }, 500).addClass('showDrawer').removeClass('hideDrawer');
        }
    }

    function getNotifications() {
        var monthAbbreviations = [
            "Jan",
            "Feb",
            "Mar",
            "Apr",
            "May",
            "Jun",
            "Jul",
            "Aug",
            "Sep",
            "Oct",
            "Nov",
            "Dec"
        ];

        window.fetch("https://services.gazette.com/TNCMS/notifications/")
            .then(function(response) {
                response
                    .text()
                    .then(function(responseData) {
                        responseData = ((typeof(responseData) === 'string') ? JSON.parse(responseData) : responseData);

                        if (typeof responseData.response != 'undefined') {
                            var notifications           = responseData.response;
                            var displayNotifications    = '';

                            $.each(notifications, function(notificationNumber, notification) {
                                var notificationSegments    = notification.included_segments;
                                var notificationSegment     = '';

                                for (var i = 0; i < notificationSegments.length; i++) {
                                    if (notificationSegments[i] == 'All') {
                                        notificationSegments[i] = 'Critical Alert - All Users';
                                    }
                                    if (notificationSegments[i] !== null) {
                                        if (notificationSegment == '') {
                                            notificationSegment = notificationSegments[i];
                                        } else {
                                            notificationSegment += ', ' + notificationSegments[i];
                                        }
                                    }
                                }

                                var notificationURL = notification.url;
                                if (notificationURL == "") {
                                    notificationURL = "https://www.gazette.com";
                                }

                                var notificationHeader = notification.headings.en;
                                if (notificationHeader.length > 40) {
                                    notificationHeader = notificationHeader.substring(0, 40) + '...';
                                }

                                var notificationContent = notification.contents.en;
                                if (notificationContent.length > 125) {
                                    notificationContent = notificationContent.substring(0, 125) + '...';
                                }

                                var notificationSentTime    = new Date(0);
                                notificationSentTime.setUTCSeconds(notification.send_after);
                                var notificationSentTimeHours   = notificationSentTime.getHours();
                                var notificationSentTimeAMPM    = '';
                                if (notificationSentTimeHours >= 12) {
                                    notificationSentTimeHours   = (notificationSentTimeHours - 12).toString();
                                    notificationSentTimeAMPM    = 'pm';
                                } else if (notificationSentTimeHours == 0) {
                                    notificationSentTimeHours   = '12';
                                    notificationSentTimeAMPM    = 'am';
                                } else {
                                    notificationSentTimeHours   = notificationSentTimeHours.toString();
                                    notificationSentTimeAMPM    = 'am';
                                }

                                displayNotifications    += '<a href="' + notificationURL + '" class="notification-item-link">';
                                displayNotifications    += '<div class="notification-item">';
                                displayNotifications    += '<div class="notification-item-header">';
                                displayNotifications    += notificationHeader;
                                displayNotifications    += '<' + '/' + 'div>';
                                displayNotifications    += '<div class="notification-segment">';
                                displayNotifications    += notificationSegment;
                                displayNotifications    += '<' + '/' + 'div>';
                                displayNotifications    += notificationContent;
                                displayNotifications    += '<span class="notification-item-sent">';
                                displayNotifications    += monthAbbreviations[notificationSentTime.getMonth()];
                                displayNotifications    += ' ' + notificationSentTime.getDate().toString();
                                displayNotifications    += ', ' + notificationSentTime.getFullYear().toString();
                                displayNotifications    += ' ' + notificationSentTimeHours;
                                displayNotifications    += ':' + notificationSentTime.getMinutes().toString();
                                displayNotifications    += notificationSentTimeAMPM;
                                displayNotifications    += '<' + '/' + 'span>';
                                displayNotifications    += '<' + '/' + 'div>';
                                displayNotifications    += '<' + '/' + 'a>';
                            });

                            $('#pushNotifications').html(displayNotifications);
                        } else {
                            $('#pushNotifications').html("Data Error");
                            console.error('[OneSignal] API Notifications - Data Error in responseData.response');
                            console.error(responseData.response);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(function(error) {
                        $('#pushNotifications').html("Data Error");
                        console.error('[OneSignal] API Notifications - Data Error in responseData');
                        console.error(error);
                    })
            })
            .catch(function(error) {
                $('#pushNotifications').html("Cannot get data");
                console.error('[OneSignal] API Notifications - Unable to get data.');
            });
    }

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
        getNotifications();
        gazetteNotificationsBell.show();
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.gazette-bell-launcher-button', function() {
        toggleDrawer();
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.pushNavButton', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var pushedButton    = $(this);

        // Push Notifications Nav Buttons
        $('.pushNavButton').removeClass('active').removeClass('disabled');
        pushedButton.addClass('active');

        // Push Notifications Content
        var pushNavContent = pushedButton.attr('href').substring(1);
        $('.push-notifications-content > div').hide();
        $('#' + pushNavContent).show();

        return false;
    });
          </script>
         </div>

3bKoMuGUc4eKlCFLMu4494HePLZvyPVkHL3g48wGsO64VAU+k2JiY1SKhUL4YkldMiRKKPWY6sFihALrG9lWDNnREQ5I3GVzqDrTV27SxVKhdWNkkWJQUR46/ARNj7+NM9u28HR6TYPbnqSW39/L9/+2c2k3cOsHpZ6vRmyUKpQeKmbhAJwleGZUigrV4oq5zQKVjcc65p5DRxgoojqyuC81O1ZGJhAZifZ/sKLADzyxNOUvmTLjl1s3r6T3933EHle8OQzf+frP/gJ7Vd3sSipZLXlLa8TmTJkQiqQeSVK5zUKrchz1eIuHiFC2ZtZXp5NcCrzftsvXX1dr4wz7r79Fp7ZuoOH77qZa790Hd1uNwSmifDq6z1cWbKo2eArX/06qy65Atk9rbpjKiRGESWWECT9DYIrA8uXjvQYi8t6lLRG2d+zvNxJyLzUw5IbYC+lZNumv/Cn++4ny3MuuuA8Xty9h7gqBIOtWv/x3pNlPb5zw/cwS9O5dCJAOqAtqlESgTMTNwAuzBWlCqtSx0WtjEbkMaLYgYlOVdmx5VkefPAhCueI47gGN1gMjm3RjDF4FZLeFKZlg0YUDfrROZAiIXkb4NxmgTFRDTyKDMYYkqEhVjRgfSsnEuh4E/QqQtbr8NA9f2C63SGKQtrqMycnac+stXz0A+/HGIHVrcBG3z39Iq9VRTknLRhNI/bsP0CaJCRJzAsvvcIXv3kjP/zV7bz86j5WjQ5xyUhJKwoHNQY2P/4oEwffwA4wdipPUTg+eOVljC9ZHAAub0AahWzmqtTQjDwjtmTEela2DJu3Ps9nvnYD9298jLcmp/jVnX9kx4sv8/CmJ/nsN77LF677Pv/cuZ31rR6NCLJexhMP30+cJMGNpwhOVcmd4zPXfowktmFwdx52HYU9bcUK86a4dww7Drywhet/ejN5XpDECevXncffnttJmiRB5CL4sqSX5axfu4ZrP/FJtr+yn6c2Pky0QFe08Hwd3F4Ujsvf/U5+eeP1LBtfgnivKgKHM9h2WInxTJehhoxaz8yLm7np13cwOXUUYwyqinMlcbzwxq4sybOMOLbEccLpPF6VJI758be+xsev/mA1uFfcj6XK2S2hXZpqHoHX/rGFW357F4cmpzDG1FF3InAANopoNptYG58WuH66uXrDFXxkwxVzwSID9yhrFylTmXAog727/8k9v7mNiamjdeSdziMip73mnJUruO7Ln6eRpnWnYwZn0kiEy8ahZTz33Xkbh/9LcKf7qCpxknDzj27grOXLFr6b6YO0Bt4/XtAwCmI4hQvY0wc0AKwP7p5bf866c1cfV1nM8dO90khT7vv1TVzxnksQEbz3/1egUgWEAqtXruDe237BheevmTc/v/0FZvXDTrfH7Xf/mQcefYzJqSPE1v5X2jrWtnMljcYQV2+4kuu+/DnOWr5sQXAnuQLWemh6duvz3L/xMR554inUe5I4rlPOyQDPXQQpReHInWPDe9/Dp675GFdveB9Dafq/XKLPATg60+alV17lgUcfY9Nfn2Hq6DRDaYKNorrgH6sf7z1l6cmLgshGfOjKy/n0NR/lXRdfyLKxJSfsZk4ZIAvcXDnnmG7Psnn7Tp7avIXndv2LN948ROmVqGrfvSreK2cuHePCdedz1WXv5sNXXs74ksWhfPXvaU7BA/8BDKKUNKci5HUAAAAASUVORK5CYII=')}
          </style>
          <script>
           /**
 * Combo widgets
 *
 * @author Anthony Diaz, CSGazette
 */

// Nested ready state here is not needed until we go completely async, but this allows the rotators to register when the DOM is ready and will wait until jQuery becomes available.

$('document').ready(function(){
    try {
        if (window.self !== window.top) {
            return;
        }
    } catch (e) {
        return;
    }

		//Format HTML to compatible specification
    $('*:not(.flexHoverWidgetSwapperWidget) + .flexHoverWidgetSwapperWidget').before('<div class="flexHoverWidgetSwapper"><div class="flexHoverSwapperTransitionContainer"><div class="flexHoverSwapperWidgetsContainer">');
        $('.flexHoverWidgetSwapperWidget').appendTo('.flexHoverSwapperWidgetsContainer');

         $('.flexHoverWidgetSwapper').each(function(index, element){
            var $this = $(element),

            /**
             * LS UID for remembering selection state of the widget
             *
             * @type {string}
             */
            uid = 'CSGWidgets_WidgetHoverSwapper-',

            /**
             * The loaded value from LS, if any
             */
            lsVal,

            /**
             * The container for all sub widgets.  This element is translated to "swap" widgets in and out
             */
            $transitionContainer,

            /**
             * The reference to the available widgets to this swapper
             */
            $widgets,

            /**
             * The reference to the buttons container
             */
            $buttonsContainer,

            /**
             * The reference to the buttons for event handling
             */
            $buttons,

            /**
             * Internal counter
             */
            i = 0,

            /**
             * Internal counter limitation
             */
            j,

            /**
             * The reference to the hover timeout, used to debounce hover operations to prevent accidental changes
             */
            hoverTimer,

            /**
             * Storage variable for classname operations
             */
            className,

            /**
             * Storage variable for classname operations
             */
            classNameSets,

            /**
             * Internal counter for classname operations
             */
            classNameSet,

            initializationCompleted = false,

            /**
             * Snaps the widget swapper to the specified index based on the hover timer firing or a click
             *
             * @param $element - The specific element that fired the snap
             */
            swapWidgetToIndex = function($element) {
                $buttons.removeClass('active');
                $element.addClass('active');

                $transitionContainer.attr('style', 'transform:translate(-' + $element.attr('data-hover-swapper-index') + '00%);-webkit-transform:translate(-' + $element.attr('data-hover-swapper-index') + '00%);');

                // Now set the LS cache for this setting
                localStorage.setItem(uid, $element.attr('data-hover-swapper-id'));

                if (initializationCompleted) {
                    // Send the tracking
                    setTimeout(function (widgetTitle) {
                        var bodyClassID = $('body')[0].className;

                        if (bodyClassID.indexOf(' ') > -1) {
                            bodyClassID = bodyClassID.split(' ')[0];
                        }

                        ga('send', 'event', 'widgetSwapper_Hover_' + bodyClassID, 'selectionMade', widgetTitle);
                    }, 0, $element.attr('data-hover-swapper-id'));
                }
            };

            // Prepare the button container
            $this.prepend('<div class="hoverSwapperWidgetButtonsContainer">');

            // Bind the remaining containers and index the widgets
            $transitionContainer = $($this.find('.flexHoverSwapperWidgetsContainer')[0]);
            $widgets = $this.find('.widget');
            $buttonsContainer = $this.find('.hoverSwapperWidgetButtonsContainer');

            // Get the length of the widgets list so we can loop through them all
            j = $widgets.length;

            for (i; i < j; i++) {
                className = '';

                classNameSets = $widgets[i].className.split(' ');

                for (classNameSet in classNameSets) {
                    if (classNameSets[classNameSet].indexOf('widget-icon-') === 0) {
                        className = className + ((className) ? ' ' : '') + classNameSets[classNameSet].replace('widget-icon-', '');
                        uid = uid + '-' + className;
                    }
                }

                $buttonsContainer.append('<div class="hoverSwapperButton ' + className + ((i == 0) ? ' active' : '') +  '" data-hover-swapper-index="' + i + '" data-hover-swapper-id="' + className + '">')
            }

            $buttons = $this.find('.hoverSwapperButton');

            // Attach events
            $buttons.on('mouseover', function(){
                if (hoverTimer !== null) {
                    clearTimeout(hoverTimer);
                }

                hoverTimer = setTimeout(swapWidgetToIndex, 250, $(this));
            });
            $buttons.on('mouseout', function(){
                if (hoverTimer !== null) {
                    clearTimeout(hoverTimer);
                }
            });
            $buttons.on('click tap touch', function () {
                if (hoverTimer !== null) {
                    clearTimeout(hoverTimer);
                }

                swapWidgetToIndex($(this));
            });

            // Grab our LS cached value and snap to the proper pane if one was chosen
            lsVal = localStorage.getItem(uid);

            // Check LS and see if a widget with this ID has saved a config
            if ((uid != 'CSGWidgets_WidgetSwapper-') && lsVal) {
                $this.find('[data-hover-swapper-id="' + lsVal + '"]').click();
            }

            initializationCompleted = true;
        });
});
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>

       <div class="col-md-12">

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.tncmsTrackEvent));
            });
        });

            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                var dmpData = el.dataset.tncmsTrackDmp;

        });

  <script>
   /*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                } /*]]>*/
  </script>
